      "import express from \"express\";\nimport path from \"path\";\nimport { createServer as createViteServer } from \"vite\";\nimport { GoogleGenAI, Type } from \"@google/genai\";\nimport dotenv from \"dotenv\";\n\n// Import Elton Boehnen canonical validation and schema engines\nimport { validateDocument, validateString, BEJSONSchema } from \"./server/bejson\";\n\ndotenv.config();\n\nconst ai = new GoogleGenAI({\n  apiKey: process.env.GEMINI_API_KEY || \"\",\n  httpOptions: {\n    headers: {\n      'User-Agent': 'aistudio-build',\n    }\n  }\n});\n\nasync function startServer() {\n  const app = express();\n  const PORT = 3000;\n\n  // Use JSON limit large enough for zip file structure text\n  app.use(express.json({ limit: \"50mb\" }));\n\n  // Helper function to query Gemini with dynamic model selection and custom config profiles\n  const queryGemini = async (\n    prompt: string, \n    jsonSchema?: any, \n    model: string = \"gemini-2.5-flash\",\n    systemInstruction?: string,\n    temperature?: number,\n    maxOutputTokens?: number,\n    retries: number = 4\n  ): Promise<string> => {\n    const config: any = {};\n    if (jsonSchema) {\n      config.responseMimeType = \"application/json\";\n      config.responseSchema = jsonSchema;\n    }\n    if (systemInstruction) {\n      config.systemInstruction = systemInstruction;\n    }\n    if (typeof temperature === 'number') {\n      config.temperature = temperature;\n    }\n    if (typeof maxOutputTokens === 'number') {\n      config.maxOutputTokens = maxOutputTokens;\n    }\n    \n    const targetModel = model || \"gemini-3.5-flash\";\n    \n    let attempt = 0;\n    while (attempt < retries) {\n      try {\n        const response = await ai.models.generateContent({\n          model: targetModel,\n          contents: prompt,\n          config\n        });\n        return response.text || \"\";\n      } catch (err: any) {\n        attempt++;\n        const errMsg = typeof err?.message === 'string' ? err.message : JSON.stringify(err);\n        const isRetryable = errMsg.includes('503') || errMsg.includes('429') || errMsg.includes('UNAVAILABLE') || errMsg.includes('high demand') || errMsg.includes('overloaded');\n        \n        if (attempt >= retries || !isRetryable) {\n          if (errMsg.includes('503') || errMsg.includes('high demand') || errMsg.includes('UNAVAILABLE')) {\n            throw new Error(\"The selected AI model is currently experiencing high demand. Please try again in a few moments or select a different model in the settings.\");\n          }\n          if (errMsg.includes('429') || errMsg.includes('RESOURCE_EXHAUSTED') || errMsg.includes('quota')) {\n            throw new Error(\"The selected AI model's API quota or rate limit has been exceeded. Please try again later or swap to a different model.\");\n          }\n          throw new Error(err.message || \"Unknown GenAI API error\");\n        }\n        await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, 1000 * Math.pow(2, attempt - 1)));\n      }\n    }\n    return \"\";\n  };\n\n  // API Route: Validate BEJSON raw text or structure\n  app.post(\"/api/bejson/validate\", async (req, res) => {\n    try {\n      const { jsonText, document } = req.body;\n      let result;\n      if (jsonText) {\n        result = validateString(jsonText);\n      } else if (document) {\n        result = validateDocument(document);\n      } else {\n        return res.status(400).json({ error: \"Missing 'jsonText' or 'document' in body.\" });\n      }\n      res.json({ result });\n    } catch (e: any) {\n      res.status(500).json({ error: e.message || \"Validation routine failed.\" });\n    }\n  });\n\n  // API Route: Extract BEJSON Schema Layout\n  app.post(\"/api/bejson/extract-schema\", async (req, res) => {\n    try {\n      const { document } = req.body;\n      if (!document) {\n        return res.status(400).json({ error: \"Missing 'document' parameter.\" });\n      }\n      const schema = BEJSONSchema.extract(document);\n      res.json({ schema });\n    } catch (e: any) {\n      res.status(500).json({ error: e.message || \"Failed to extract schema metadata.\" });\n    }\n  });\n\n  // API Route: Generate 25 Interview Questions\n  app.post(\"/api/gemini/generate-questions\", async (req, res) => {\n    try {\n      const { projectName, userName, userEmail, contextText, model, systemInstruction, temperature, maxOutputTokens } = req.body;\n      \n      const prompt = `You are playing the role of an expert software interviewer. \n      Analyze the following project structure and code context to come up with a series of exactly 25 thoughtful questions \n      to interview the creator of the project.\n      The project is named \"${projectName}\", created by \"${userName}\" (${userEmail}).\n      \n      Project Context: \n      \\n${contextText}\\n\n      \n      Please return exactly 25 highly relevant, inspiring questions list. The questions should focus on:\n      - Inspiration and core objectives\n      - Designing choices and architectural trade-offs\n      - Issues/bugs encountered, expectations set or missed\n      - User guides, setup instructions, and package utility.\n      \n      Format your response as a valid JSON array of 25 strings containing the questions only. Let's make it very inspiring.`;\n\n      const schema = {\n        type: Type.ARRAY,\n        items: {\n          type: Type.STRING\n        }\n      };\n\n      const resultText = await queryGemini(prompt, schema, model, systemInstruction, temperature, maxOutputTokens);\n      const questions = JSON.parse(resultText || \"[]\");\n      res.json({ questions });\n    } catch (e: any) {\n      res.status(500).json({ error: e.message || \"Failed to generate interview questions\" });\n    }\n  });\n\n  // API Route: Generate specific part of Multi-Part Documentation\n  app.post(\"/api/gemini/generate-part\", async (req, res) => {\n    try {\n      const { partNumber, partTitle, projectName, userName, interviewQnA, contextText, model, totalParts, systemInstruction, temperature, maxOutputTokens } = req.body;\n      \n      const totalPartsCount = totalParts || 5;\n      const isExhaustive = totalPartsCount > 8;\n\n      const prompt = `You are a developer documentation assistant writing a multi-part guidebook for \"${projectName}\" created by \"${userName}\".\n      This is Part ${partNumber}: \"${partTitle}\" of a ${totalPartsCount}-part comprehensive documentation.\n      \n      Below are the interview answers from the creator of the project:\n      ${JSON.stringify(interviewQnA, null, 2)}\n      \n      And here is the project context/codebase structure of the imported archive:\n      ${contextText}\n      \n      CRITICAL DIRECTIVE ON AUTHOR RECOGNITION & CREDIT:\n      You MUST inspect the imported project's codebase context (especially package.json \"author\" or \"contributors\" fields, code headers, comments, or the developer info: \"${userName}\") to recognize the original project creator/author. \n      In this documentation part, you MUST properly credit the author/creator in an elegant, professional manner. If this is Part 1 or Part ${totalPartsCount}, include a dedicated \"Author & Credits\" header or summary acknowledging the original developer, their contributions, and their email if mentioned.\n\n      ${isExhaustive ? `\n      CRITICAL DIRECTIVE - EXHAUSTIVE TECHNICAL DEPTH:\n      Because you are writing an extensive ${totalPartsCount}-part documentation (which is greater than 8 parts), you MUST provide exhaustive technical details.\n      - Go extremely deep into implementation patterns, code snippets, variables, components structure, and configuration states.\n      - Do NOT summarize or use placeholder items. Describe the mechanics of the codebase with high-fidelity, high-precision engineering explanations.\n      - Index and outline functions/subsystems meticulously.\n      ` : ''}\n\n      Please draft an extensive, highly technical, and descriptive markdown explanation for Part ${partNumber}: \"${partTitle}\" based directly on their actual answers. Be thorough, use clean markdown, and avoid generic fluff. Ensure you write deep technical descriptions. Include file names and references.`;\n\n      const resultText = await queryGemini(prompt, undefined, model, systemInstruction, temperature, maxOutputTokens);\n      res.json({ output: resultText });\n    } catch (e: any) {\n      res.status(500).json({ error: e.message || \"Failed to generate part documentation\" });\n    }\n  });\n\n  // API Route: Combine & Audit Final Document\n  app.post(\"/api/gemini/combine-and-audit\", async (req, res) => {\n    try {\n      const { combinedText, projectName, model, systemInstruction, temperature, maxOutputTokens } = req.body;\n      \n      const prompt = `You are performing a compliance and formatting audit on an extensive multi-part documentation draft for the project \"${projectName}\".\n      \n      The document is down below. Your assignment is to:\n      1. Merge it into a single, cohesive, publication-ready document.\n      2. Ensure we prefix every main section and paragraph cleanly with sequential line reference brackets, so that a reader can point to them easily (e.g. prefix paragraphs with [Line 10], [Line 20], [Line 30]... or similar indicators scattered through the text so specific lines can be easily selected).\n      3. Clean up formatting, fix typos, verify consistency.\n      4. Ensure that the original author/creator of the codebase (searched from the text, codebases, or configuration details) is prominently recognized and properly credited with a beautiful dedication section or table near the beginning or end of the document. Do not let their authorship be omitted.\n      \n      Document content:\n      ${combinedText}\n      \n      Return the audited and formatted document in rich Markdown with bracketed reference line indicators.`;\n\n      const resultText = await queryGemini(prompt, undefined, model, systemInstruction, temperature, maxOutputTokens);\n      res.json({ output: resultText });\n    } catch (e: any) {\n      res.status(500).json({ error: e.message || \"Failed to audit and finalise document\" });\n    }\n  });\n\n  // API Route: Rewrite / Revise Chunk\n  app.post(\"/api/gemini/rewrite-chunk\", async (req, res) => {\n    try {\n      const { originalText, comment, model, systemInstruction, temperature, maxOutputTokens } = req.body;\n      \n      const prompt = `You are a documentation editor.\n      A developer has asked to rewrite/revise the following section of their project guide.\n      \n      Original Paragraph/Section:\n      \"\"\"\n      ${originalText}\n      \"\"\"\n      \n      User Instructions / Comments for Rewrite:\n      \"${comment}\"\n      \n      Please regenerate this segment incorporating their specific comments perfectly while maintaining a professional, descriptive technical style. Preserve any line bracket references if appropriate, and maintain accurate author/creator credits if referenced.`;\n\n      const resultText = await queryGemini(prompt, undefined, model, systemInstruction, temperature, maxOutputTokens);\n      res.json({ output: resultText });\n    } catch (e: any) {\n      res.status(500).json({ error: e.message || \"Failed to rewrite chunk\" });\n    }\n  });\n\n  // API Route: Generate Timeline Plan\n  app.post(\"/api/gemini/generate-plan\", async (req, res) => {\n    try {\n      const { prompt, model, systemInstruction, temperature, maxOutputTokens } = req.body;\n      \n      const schema = {\n        type: Type.ARRAY,\n        items: {\n          type: Type.OBJECT,\n          properties: {\n            number: { type: Type.INTEGER },\n            title: { type: Type.STRING },\n            instruction: { type: Type.STRING }\n          },\n          required: [\"number\", \"title\", \"instruction\"]\n        }\n      };\n\n      const resultText = await queryGemini(prompt, schema, model, systemInstruction, temperature, maxOutputTokens);\n      res.json({ output: resultText });\n    } catch (e: any) {\n      res.status(500).json({ error: e.message || \"Failed to generate plan\" });\n    }\n  });\n\n  // API Route: Generate ReadMe (Single-shot fallback)\n  app.post(\"/api/gemini/generate-docs\", async (req, res) => {\n    try {\n      const { prompt, contextText, model, systemInstruction, temperature, maxOutputTokens } = req.body;\n      \n      const fullPrompt = `${prompt}\n\nCRITICAL DIRECTIVE ON AUTHOR RECOGNITION & CREDIT:\nYou MUST search the codebase information below (especially package.json \"author\", \"contributors\", or developer signatures in files) to find the original author/creator's name, email, or credentials.\nYou MUST prominently see out and credit the original author properly in the generated ReadMe/Documentation file under an elegant, dedicated \"Author & Credits\" header or banner near the top or footer, stating they are the original programmer of this codebase. Do not omit this recognition.\n\nContext codebase information:\n${contextText}\n\nPlease generate a very detailed and extensive markdown document based on the requirements above.`;\n\n      const resultText = await queryGemini(fullPrompt, undefined, model, systemInstruction, temperature, maxOutputTokens);\n      res.json({ output: resultText });\n    } catch (e: any) {\n      res.status(500).json({ error: e.message || \"Failed to generate ReadMe docs\" });\n    }\n  });\n\n  // API Route: Generate Landing Page FAQ\n  app.post(\"/api/gemini/generate-faq\", async (req, res) => {\n    try {\n      const { interviewQnA, contextText, model, systemInstruction, temperature, maxOutputTokens } = req.body;\n      \n      const fullPrompt = `Based on the following project context and the detailed interview with the creator, generate a comprehensive, professional FAQ section for the app's landing page.       "# Changelog\n\nAll notable changes to this project will be documented in this file.\n\n---\n\n## [1.3.9] - 2026-06-05\n\n### Changed\n- **Optimized BEJSON Chunker Architect Profile**: Added precise context and comprehensive guidelines to the system preset instruction matching the Elton Boehnen BEJSON 104db specifications.\n- **Spreadsheet Analogy Integration**: Added direct explanations relating Fields to column headers, Values to positional aligned rows, and the `Record_Type_Parent` discriminator to combining multiple spreadsheet pages.\n- **V1.3.9 Version Bump**: Synchronized metadata with package configuration and bumped editor version.\n\n---\n\n## [1.3.8] - 2026-06-05\n\n### Added\n- **Interactive Chunker AI Playground Tab**: Integrated a dedicated \"Chunker Chat (Test)\" workspace under the sidebar. Allows full chat conversation with Chunker AI to evaluate output formatting rules.\n- **Format & Schema Tester Unit**: Implemented a canonical BEJSON-104db validation checker matching CLI Chunker v1.6.0 requirements. Offers detailed structural reports on Fields mapping and positional conformity.\n- **Virtual File Rebuilder Explorer**: Implemented an in-memory virtual unchunking emulator showing live expandable folder directories from generated BEJSON Values entries.\n- **One-click Package Import**: Equipped Clint Developer with a utility shortcut to load currently imported codebase ZIP references straight into the test playground.\n\n---\n\n## [1.3.7] - 2026-06-05\n\n### Changed\n- **Graceful Zip Exception Handling**: Intercepted header-reading and corrupted ZIP exceptions (e.g., \"Corrupted zip: can't find end of central directory\") inside the `ZipUploader` load routine. Stored errors in React state and displayed them gracefully in-app using the `StatusIndicator` component.\n- **Removed window.alert**: Eliminated the potentially blocking and disruptive browser native alert dialogs during parsing failures, adhering to platform constraints.\n- Bumped app engine and editor version parameters to `v1.3.7`.\n\n---\n\n## [1.3.6] - 2026-06-05\n\n### Changed\n- **Relocated Status Indicators**: Removed the detached top-of-panel status bar and embedded compact, single-row status blocks directly inside the working directive boxes (underneath the active build/send buttons).\n- **Refined Status Layout**: Positioned the glowing, color-coded live system status light directly before the uppercase label text (e.g., `IDLE`, `TRANSMITTING`) on the primary line.\n- Bumped app engine version to `v1.3.6` across configuration parameters.\n\n---\n\n## [1.3.5] -       "import React, { useState } from 'react';\nimport JSZip from 'jszip';\nimport { Menu, Package, FileText, MessageSquare, X, Brain, Download, Sparkles, CheckCircle2, User, Cpu, Database } from './components/DocumentationTool';\nimport { AIProfilesTool, PRESETS } from './components/AIProfilesTool';\nimport { ChunkerChatTool } from './components/ChunkerChatTool';\nimport { LibraryTool } from './components/LibraryTool';\nimport { ToolType, AIProfile } from './types';\nimport { cn } from './lib/utils';\n\n\nexport default function App() {\n  const [sidebarOpen, setSidebarOpen] = useState(false);\n  const [activeView, setActiveView] = useState<'analyzer' | 'profiles' | 'chunkerChat' | 'library'>('analyzer');\n  const [activeProfile, setActiveProfile] = useState<AIProfile | null>(null);\n  const [selectedTool, setSelectedTool] = useState<ToolType>('single_prompt');\n  \n  // Codebase Zip States\n  const [zipFiles, setZipFiles] = useState<string[]>([]);\n  const [zipContextText, setZipContextText] = useState('');\n  const [jszipInstance, setJszipInstance] = useState<JSZip | null>(null);\n  const [zipFileName, setZipFileName] = useState('project.zip');\n  const [extraFilesAdded, setExtraFilesAdded] = useState<string[]>([]);\n  const [importExpanded, setImportExpanded] = useState(true);\n\n  // AI model selection default\n  const [selectedModel, setSelectedModel] = useState('gemini-3.5-flash');\n\n  // Load app state\n  React.useEffect(() => {\n    const saved = localStorage.getItem('packcraft_app_state');\n    if (saved) {\n      try {\n        const parsed = JSON.parse(saved);\n        if (parsed.activeView) setActiveView(parsed.activeView);\n        if (parsed.selectedTool) setSelectedTool(parsed.selectedTool);\n        if (parsed.selectedModel) setSelectedModel(parsed.selectedModel);\n        if (parsed.activeProfileId) {\n          const profiles = getProfiles();\n          const p = profiles.find(p => p.id === parsed.activeProfileId);\n          if (p) setActiveProfile(p);\n        }\n        if (parsed.zipFileName) setZipFileName(parsed.zipFileName);\n        if (parsed.zipFiles) setZipFiles(parsed.zipFiles);\n        if (parsed.zipContextText) setZipContextText(parsed.zipContextText);\n        if (parsed.extraFilesAdded) setExtraFilesAdded(parsed.extraFilesAdded);\n      } catch (e) {\n        // ignore\n      }\n    }\n  }, []);\n\n  // Save app state\n  React.useEffect(() => {\n    try {\n      localStorage.setItem('packcraft_app_state', JSON.stringify({\n        activeView,\n        selectedTool,\n        selectedModel,\n        activeProfileId: activeProfile?.id,\n        zipFileName,\n        zipFiles,\n        zipContextText,\n        extraFilesAdded\n      }));\n    } catch (e) {\n      // If quota exceeded (large zip context), save without it\n      try {\n        localStorage.setItem('packcraft_app_state', JSON.stringify({\n          activeView,\n          selectedTool,\n          selectedModel,\n          activeProfileId: activeProfile?.id\n        }));\n      } catch (e2) {}\n    }\n  }, [activeView, selectedTool, selectedModel, activeProfile, zipFileName, zipFiles, zipContextText, extraFilesAdded]);\n\n  React.useEffect(() => {\n    const handleNav = (e: any) => {\n      const { view, tool } = e.detail;\n      setActiveView(view);\n      if (tool) setSelectedTool(tool);\n    };\n    window.addEventListener('packcraft:navigate', handleNav);\n    return () => window.removeEventListener('packcraft:navigate', handleNav);\n  }, []);\n\n  // Load profiles from local storage or fallback to PRESETS\n  const getProfiles = (): AIProfile[] => {\n    const saved = localStorage.getItem('packcraft_ai_profiles');\n    if (saved) {\n      try {\n        return JSON.parse(saved);\n      } catch (e) {\n        return PRESETS;\n      }\n    }\n    return PRESETS;\n  };\n\n  // Helper to retrieve the current effective profile for a given view or tool\n  const getEffectiveProfile = (): AIProfile | null => {\n    const profiles = getProfiles();\n    \n    // Determine the task string corresponding to the current screen/tool\n    let currentTask = 'none';\n    if (activeView === 'chunkerChat') {\n      currentTask = 'chunker';\n    } else if (activeView === 'analyzer') {\n      if (selectedTool === 'single_prompt') {\n        currentTask = 'readme';\n      } else if (selectedTool === 'multi_prompt') {\n        currentTask = 'documentation';\n      } else if (selectedTool === 'interview') {\n        currentTask = 'interview';\n      } else if (selectedTool === 'investigator') {\n        currentTask = 'investigate';\n      }\n    }\n\n    // If an active profile is manually set/confirmed, let's see if it maps\n    // to 'all' or specifically aligns with the current task. If so, respect manual select.\n    if (activeProfile) {\n      const isCompatible = !activeProfile.AssociatedTask || \n                           activeProfile.AssociatedTask === 'all' || \n                           activeProfile.AssociatedTask === currentTask;\n      if (isCompatible) {\n        return activeProfile;\n      }\n    }\n\n    // Otherwise, find a profile that specifically lists currentTask as its AssociatedTask\n    const specificMatch = profiles.find(p => p.AssociatedTask === currentTask);\n    if (specificMatch) return specificMatch;\n\n    // Find any profile mapped to 'all'\n    const allMatch = profiles.find(p => p.AssociatedTask === 'all');\n    if (allMatch) return allMatch;\n\n    // Fallback to presets matching the task\n    const presetMatch = PRESETS.find(p       "import React, { useState } from 'react';\nimport JSZip from 'jszip';\nimport { UploadCloud, ChevronDown, ChevronRight, FileJson } from 'lucide-react';\nimport { cn } from '../lib/utils';\nimport { StatusIndicator } from './StatusIndicator';\n\ninterface ZipUploaderProps {\n  onZipParsed: (files: string[], contextText: string, zip: JSZip, fileName: string) => void;\n  files: string[];\n}\n\nexport function ZipUploader({ onZipParsed, files }: ZipUploaderProps) {\n  const [isParsing, setIsParsing] = useState(false);\n  const [isExpanded, setIsExpanded] = useState(false);\n  const [parseError, setParseError] = useState<string | null>(null);\n\n  const handleFileUpload = async (event: React.ChangeEvent<HTMLInputElement>) => {\n    const file = event.target.files?.[0];\n    if (!file) return;\n\n    setIsParsing(true);\n    setParseError(null);\n    try {\n      const zip = await JSZip.loadAsync(file);\n      const filePaths: string[] = [];\n      let contextText = `Project File Tree:\\n`;\n\n      zip.forEach((relativePath, zipEntry) => {\n        filePaths.push(relativePath);\n        contextText += `- ${relativePath}\\n`;\n      });\n\n      // Try to glean some contents\n      const fileExtsToRead = ['.json', '.md', '.ts', '.js', '.tsx', '.jsx'];\n      let extraContext = '';\n      \n      for (const [relativePath, file] of Object.entries(zip.files)) {\n         if (file.dir) continue;\n         const isText = fileExtsToRead.some(ext => relativePath.endsWith(ext));\n         if (isText && extraContext.length < 50000) { // Limit size\n             try {\n                 const content = await file.async('string');\n                 extraContext += `\\n--- ${relativePath} ---\\n${content.substring(0, 3000)}\\n`;\n             } catch(e) {}\n         }\n      }\n\n      onZipParsed(filePaths, contextText + extraContext, zip, file.name);\n    } catch (e: any) {\n      console.warn(\"API Error caught:\", e.message);\n      setParseError(e?.message?.includes(\"Corrupted zip\") \n        ? \"The uploaded ZIP file appears to be corrupted or invalid.\" \n        : (e?.message || \"Failed to parse zip file.\"));\n      if (event.target) {\n        event.target.value = '';\n      }\n    } finally {\n      setIsParsing(false);\n    }\n  };\n\n  return (\n    <div className=\"space-y-4 font-mono text-white\">\n      <div className=\"c-card\">\n        <div className=\"c-card__header relative select-none\">\n          <span className=\"c-card__title\">\ud83d\udcc1 [01] IMPORT CODEBASE ARCHIVE ENVELOPE</span>\n        </div>\n        <div className=\"c-card__body py-2.5\">\n          <label className=\"w-full flex items-center justify-center gap-2 py-2.5 border-2 border-zinc-800 bg-[#de2626] text-white hover:bg-black transition-all cursor-pointer font-black text-xs uppercase font-mono text-center\">\n            <UploadCloud className=\"w-4 h-4 text-white shrink-0\" />\n            <span>{isParsing ? 'PARSING ENVELOPE...' : 'CHOOSE ARCHIVE ZIP'}</span>\n            <input id=\"zip-file-input\" type=\"file\" className=\"hidden\" accept=\".zip\" onChange={handleFileUpload} />\n          </label>\n          \n          {parseError && (\n            <div className=\"mt-2.5\">\n              <StatusIndicator status=\"error\" message={parseError} />\n            </div>\n          )}\n        </div>\n      </div>\n\n      {files.length > 0 && (\n        <div className=\"c-card\">\n          <button \n            onClick={() => setIsExpanded(!isExpanded)}\n            className=\"c-card__header cursor-pointer select-none\"\n            aria-expanded={isExpanded}\n          >\n            <span className=\"c-card__title flex items-center gap-2\">\n              <FileJson className=\"w-4 h-4 text-[#de2626] shrink-0\" />\n              <span>ZIP SCAN ENVELOPE CONTENTS</span>\n              <span className=\"text-[9px] px-1 bg-[#de2626] text-white font-mono font-black\">{files.length} ITEMS</span>\n            </span>\n            <span className=\"c-card__toggle\">{isExpanded ? 'CLOSE' : 'OPEN'}</span>\n          </button>\n          \n          {isExpanded && (\n            <div className=\"c-card__body bg-black/40 max-h-40 overflow-y-auto font-mono text-[9px] text-zinc-300\">\n              <div className=\"grid grid-cols-1 sm:grid-cols-2 gap-1.5 select-text\">\n                {files.map((file, i) => (\n                  <div key={i} className=\"flex items-center gap-2 p-1.5 bg-[#0a0a0a] border border-zinc-800 truncate font-mono\">\n                    <div className={cn(\"w-1.5 h-1.5 shrink-0 rounded-none bg-zinc-500\",\n                      (file.endsWith('.ts') || file.endsWith('.tsx')) && \"bg-[#de2626]\",\n                      file.endsWith('.json') && \"bg-amber-500\",\n                      file.endsWith('.md') && \"bg-white border border-zinc-700\"\n                    )}></div>\n                    <span className=\"truncate text-zinc-300\">{file}</span>\n                  </div>\n                ))}\n              </div>\n            </div>\n          )}\n        </div>\n      )}\n    </div>\n  );\n}\n",

'sending' | 'waiting_reception' | 'waiting_user' | 'compiling' | 'success' | 'error';\n\ninterface Props {\n  status: StatusType;\n  message?: string;\n  className?: string;\n  onIdleTimeout?: () => void;\n}\n\nexport function StatusIndicator({ status, message, className, onIdleTimeout }: Props) {\n  useEffect(() => {\n    if (status === 'success' && onIdleTimeout) {\n      const timer = setTimeout(() => {\n        onIdleTimeout();\n      }, 10000);\n      return () => clearTimeout(timer);\n    }\n  }, [status, onIdleTimeout]);\n\n  const config = {\n    idle: {\n      label: 'Idle',\n      color: 'bg-zinc-500',\n      textColor: 'text-zinc-200 border-zinc-800 bg-zinc-900/80',\n      icon: <Circle className=\"w-3.5 h-3.5 text-zinc-500\" />\n    },\n    sending: {\n      label: 'Sending',\n      color: 'bg-[#de2626] animate-ping',\n      textColor: 'text-white border-zinc-805 bg-[#de2626]',\n      icon: <Zap className=\"w-3.5 h-3.5 text-white animate-bounce\" />\n    },\n    waiting_reception: {\n      label: 'Received, waiting for reply',\n      color: 'bg-[#de2626] animate-pulse',\n      textColor: 'text-zinc-100 border-[#de2626] bg-[#1a1a1a]',\n      icon: <Loader2 className=\"w-3.5 h-3.5 text-[#de2626] animate-spin\" />\n    },\n    waiting_user: {\n      label: 'Waiting for reply',\n      color: 'bg-[#de2626]',\n      textColor: 'text-[#de2626] border-zinc-800 bg-[#161616]',\n      icon: <RefreshCw className=\"w-3.5 h-3.5 text-[#de2626] animate-spin\" />\n    },\n    compiling: {\n      label: 'Compiling',\n      color: 'bg-white animate-bounce',\n      textColor: 'text-white border-zinc-700 bg-zinc-950',\n      icon: <Loader2 className=\"w-3.5 h-3.5 text-white animate-spin\" />\n    },\n    success: {\n      label: 'Response received!',\n      color: 'bg-emerald-500',\n      textColor: 'text-emerald-400 border-emerald-900 bg-zinc-950',\n      icon: <CheckCircle className=\"w-3.5 h-3.5 text-emerald-500\" />\n    },\n    error: {\n      label: 'Error',\n      color: 'bg-[#de2626] animate-pulse',\n      textColor: 'text-white border-[#de2626] bg-[#de2626]',\n      icon: <Circle className=\"w-3.5 h-3.5 text-white font-bold\" />\n    }\n  };\n\n  const current = config[status] || config.idle;\n\n  return (\n    <div className={cn(\n      \"border border-zinc-800 bg-black/60 px-3 py-2 flex items-center gap-3 {current.label}\n        </span>\n        <span className=\"opacity-90 text-[10px] leading-tight select-text truncate font-semibold\">\n          {message || 'Workspace initialized.       "InterviewTool.tsx",
      "import React, { useState } from 'react';\nimport { Loader2, Send, Check, Clipboard, HelpCircle, Code, Database, Download } from 'lucide-react';\nimport Markdown from 'react-markdown';\nimport { StatusIndicator, StatusType } from './StatusIndicator';\nimport { AIProfile } from '../types';\nimport { saveToLibrary, removeFromLibrary } from '../lib/library';\nimport { cleanJsonString, buildHtmlFromJson } from '../lib/jsonHtmlBuilder';\n\ninterface Props {\n  contextText: string;\n  selectedModel: string;\n  onAddFileToZip?: (fileName: string, content: string) => void;\n  activeProfile?: AIProfile | null;\n}\n\nexport function InterviewTool({ contextText, selectedModel, onAddFileToZip, activeProfile }: Props) {\n  const getCompiledInstructions = () => {\n    if (!activeProfile) return undefined;\n    let insts = activeProfile.SystemInstruction || '';\n    if (activeProfile.customFields && activeProfile.customFields.length > 0) {\n      insts += '\\n\\n';\n      activeProfile.customFields.forEach(f => {\n        if (f.key && f.value) {\n          insts += `# ${f.key.trim()}\\n- ${f.value.trim()}\\n\\n`;\n        }\n      });\n    }\n    return insts;\n  };\n  // Status Indicator\n  const [status, setStatus] = useState<StatusType>('idle');\n  const [statusMsg, setStatusMsg] = useState('Idle. Import a zip file above to initialize.');\n\n  const [step, setStep] = useState<'details' | 'interview' | 'generating_all_parts' | 'complete'>('details');\n  const [details, setDetails] = useState({ projectName: '', userName: '', userEmail: '' });\n  const [questions, setQuestions] = useState<string[]>([]);\n  const [currentIndex, setCurrentIndex] = useState(0);\n  const [answers, setAnswers] = useState<Record<number, string>>({});\n  const [currentAnswer, setCurrentAnswer] = useState('');\n\n  // Generation Stages\n  const [docsParts, setDocsParts] = useState<string[]>([]);\n  const [currentPartGenerating, setCurrentPartGenerating] = useState(0);\n  const [finalAuditedDocs, setFinalAuditedDocs] = useState('');\n  \n  // FAQ Section State\n  const [faqOutput, setFaqOutput] = useState('');\n  const [generatingFaq, setGeneratingFaq] = useState(false);\n\n  // Precision Chunk select/rewrite\n  const [selectedParagraph, setSelectedParagraph] = useState('');\n  const [revisionComment, setRevisionComment] = useState('');\n  const [isRevising, setIsRevising] = useState(false);\n  const [copied, setCopied] = useState(false);\n\n  // Foldable states\n  const [infoFolded, setInfoFolded] = useState(false);\n  const [resultFolded, setResultFolded] = useState(false);\n\n  // Load state from local storage on mount\n  React.useEffect(() => {\n    const savedState = localStorage.getItem('packcraft_interview_state');\n    if (savedState) {\n      try {\n        const parsed = JSON.parse(savedState);\n        if (parsed.step) setStep(parsed.step);\n        if (parsed.details) setDetails(parsed.details);\n        if (parsed.questions) setQuestions(parsed.questions);\n        if (parsed.currentIndex !== undefined) setCurrentIndex(parsed.currentIndex);\n        if (parsed.answers) setAnswers(parsed.answers);\n        if (parsed.currentAnswer) setCurrentAnswer(parsed.currentAnswer);\n        if (parsed.docsParts) setDocsParts(parsed.docsParts);\n        if (parsed.currentPartGenerating !== undefined) setCurrentPartGenerating(parsed.currentPartGenerating);\n        if (parsed.finalAuditedDocs) setFinalAuditedDocs(parsed.finalAuditedDocs);\n        if (parsed.faqOutput) setFaqOutput(parsed.faqOutput);\n      } catch (e) {\n        console.warn(\"Failed to load interview state\", e);\n      }\n    }\n  }, []);\n\n  // Save state tracking\n  React.useEffect(() => {\n    const stateToSave = {\n      step,\n      details,\n      questions,\n      currentIndex,\n      answers,\n      currentAnswer,\n      docsParts,\n      currentPartGenerating,\n      finalAuditedDocs,\n      faqOutput,\n    };\n    localStorage.setItem('packcraft_interview_state', JSON.stringify(stateToSave));\n  }, [step, details, questions, currentIndex, answers, currentAnswer, docsParts, currentPartGenerating, finalAuditedDocs, faqOutput]);\n\n  const startInterview = async () => {\n    if (!contextText) {\n      alert(\"Please import a project zip folder first to specify context.\");\n      return;\n    }\n    if (!details.projectName || !details.userName) {\n      alert(\"Please specify the Project Name and Creator Name details!\");\n      return;\n    }\n    \n    setStatus('sending');\n    setStatusMsg('Drafting 25 tailored software interview questions from your codebase structure...');\n    \n    try {\n      const res = await fetch('/api/gemini/generate-questions', {\n        method: 'POST',\n        headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },\n        body: JSON.stringify({ \n          ...details, \n          contextText, \n          model: selectedModel,\n          systemInstruction: getCompiledInstructions(),\n          temperature: activeProfile?.Creativity,\n          maxOutputTokens: activeProfile?.MaxResponseTokens\n        })\n      });\n      const data = await res.json();\n      if (!res.ok || data.error) throw new Error(data.error || `HTTP Error: ${res.status}`);\n      if (data.questions && data.questions.length > 0) {\n        setQuestions(data.questions);\n        setStep('interview');\n        setStatus('waiting_user');\n        setStatusMsg('AI Interrogator ready. Please respond to the questions.');\n      } else {\n        throw new Error(data.error || \"No questions came back.\");\n      }\n    } catch (e: any) {\n      \n      setStatus('error');\n      setStatusMsg(`Failure initializing interview: ${e.message}`);\n    }\n  };\n\n  const handleNextQuestion = () => {\n    setAnswers(prev => ({ ...prev, [currentIndex]: currentAnswer }));\n    setCurrentAnswer('');\n    \n    if (currentIndex < questions.length - 1) {\n      setCurrentIndex(currentIndex + 1);\n      setStatus('waiting_user');\n      setStatusMsg(`Waiting responder answers to Question ${currentIndex + 2}...`);\n    } else {\n      compileFivePartDocumentation({ ...answers, [currentIndex]: currentAnswer });\n    }\n  };\n\n  const compileFivePartDocumentation = async (completedAnswers: Record<number, string>) => {\n    setStep('generating_all_parts');\n    setStatus('waiting_reception');\n    setStatusMsg('Writing document breakdown Part 1 of 5 (Overview)...');\n\n    const qna = questions.map((q, i) => ({ question: q, answer: completedAnswers[i] || 'No answer' }));\n    const generatedParts: string[] = [];\n\n    const partsMeta = [\n      \"Inspiration, Objectives, and Scope\",\n      \"User Expectations, Audience, and Feature Coverage\",\n      \"Critical Technical Architecture & Dependency Tree Breakdown\",\n      \"Coding Impediments, Bugs Faced, and Resolutions\",\n      \"Setup, Environment configurations, and local launch manual\"\n    ];\n\n    try {\n      // Loop through all 5 parts successively\n      for (let i = 0; i < 5; i++) {\n        setCurrentPartGenerating(i + 1);\n        setStatus('waiting_reception');\n        setStatusMsg(`Compiling Part ${i + 1} of 5: \"${partsMeta[i]}\" from interview insights...`);\n        \n        const res = await fetch('/api/gemini/generate-part', {\n          method: 'POST',\n          headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },\n          body: JSON.stringify({\n            partNumber: i + 1,\n            partTitle: partsMeta[i],\n            projectName: details.projectName,\n            userName: details.userName,\n            interviewQnA: qna,\n            contextText,\n            model: selectedModel,\n            systemInstruction: getCompiledInstructions(),\n            temperature: activeProfile?.Creativity,\n            maxOutputTokens: activeProfile?.MaxResponseTokens\n          })\n        });\n        const data = await res.json();\n        if (!res.ok || data.error) throw new Error(data.error || `HTTP Error: ${res.status}`);\n        if (data.output) {\n          generatedParts.push(data.output);\n          setDocsParts([...generatedParts]);\n          \n          saveToLibrary({\n            id: `interview-incomplete-${contextText.length}`,\n            title: `Incomplete Interview Strategy (${generatedParts.length}/5)`,\n            date: new Date().toLocaleString(),\n            content: generatedParts.join('\\n\\n---\\n\\n'),\n            type: 'interview',\n            isIncomplete: true\n          });\n        } else {\n          throw new Error(`Part ${i+1} returned empty content.`);\n        }\n      }\n\n      setStatus('compiling');\n      setStatusMsg('Initiating compliance audit. Formatting bracket indices...');\n      \n      const combined = generatedParts.map((t, index) => `## Part ${index+1}: ${partsMeta[index]}\\n\\n${t}`).join('\\n\\n');\n      \n      const resAudit = await fetch('/api/gemini/combine-and-audit', {\n        method: 'POST',\n        headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },\n        body: JSON.stringify({ \n          combinedText: combined, \n          projectName: details.projectName, \n          model: selectedModel,\n          systemInstruction: getCompiledInstructions(),\n          temperature: activeProfile?.Creativity,\n          maxOutputTokens: activeProfile?.MaxResponseTokens\n        })\n      });\n      const auditData = await resAudit.json();\n      if (!resAudit.ok || auditData.error) throw new Error(auditData.error || `HTTP Error: ${resAudit.status}`);\n      if (auditData.output) {\n        setFinalAuditedDocs(auditData.output);\n        if (onAddFileToZip) {\n          onAddFileToZip('DOCUMENTATION.md', auditData.output);\n        }\n        \n        saveToLibrary({\n          id: `interview-${Date.now()}`,\n          title: 'Interview Strategy Docs',\n          date: new Date().toLocaleString(),\n          content: auditData.output,\n          type: 'interview',\n          isIncomplete: false\n        });\n        removeFromLibrary(`interview-incomplete-${contextText.length}`);\n\n        setStep('complete');\n        setStatus('success');\n        setStatusMsg('Five-part documentation successfully audited and completed! Added to your archive.');\n      } else {\n        throw new Error(auditData.error || \"Auditing process was interrupted.\");\n      }\n    } catch (e: any) {\n      \n      setStatus('error');\n      setStatusMsg(`Failure in document compilation stream: ${e.message}`);\n    }\n  };\n\n  const handleFAQGeneration = async () => {\n    setGeneratingFaq(true);\n    setStatus('sending');\n    setStatusMsg('Sourcing interview transcripts to compose app Landing Page FAQ...');\n    \n    const qna = questions.map((q, i) => ({ question: q, answer: answers[i] || 'No answer' }));\n    \n    try {\n      const res = await fetch('/api/gemini/generate-faq', {\n        method: 'POST',\n        headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },\n        body: JSON.stringify({ \n          interviewQnA: qna, \n          contextText, \n          model: selectedModel,\n          systemInstruction: getCompiledInstructions(),\n          temperature: activeProfile?.Creativity,\n          maxOutputTokens: activeProfile?.MaxResponseTokens\n        })\n      });\n      const data = await res.json();\n      if (!res.ok || data.error) throw new Error(data.error || `HTTP Error: ${res.status}`);\n      if (data.output) {\n        setFaqOutput(data.output);\n        if (onAddFileToZip) {\n          onAddFileToZip('FAQ.md', data.output);\n        }\n        setStatus('success');\n        setStatusMsg('FAQ section assembled successfully! Generated FAQ.md inside zip archive!');\n      } else {\n        throw new Error(data.error || \"FAQ returned empty.\");\n      }\n    } catch (e: any) {\n      \n      setStatus('error');\n      setStatusMsg(`FAQ error: ${e.message}`);\n    } finally {\n      setGeneratingFaq(false);\n    }\n  };\n\n  // Revision tool: Re-prompt AI with chunk instructions\n  const handleChunkRevision = async () => {\n    if (!selectedParagraph || !revisionComment.trim()) return;\n\n    setIsRevising(true);\n    setStatus('waiting_reception');\n    setStatusMsg('Sending chunk revision comments to Gemini Editor...');\n    \n    try {\n      const res = await fetch('/api/gemini/rewrite-chunk', {\n        method: 'POST',\n        headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },\n        body: JSON.stringify({ \n          originalText: selectedParagraph, \n          comment: revisionComment, \n          model: selectedModel,\n          systemInstruction: getCompiledInstructions(),\n          temperature: activeProfile?.Creativity,\n          maxOutputTokens: activeProfile?.MaxResponseTokens\n        })\n      });\n      const data = await res.json();\n      if (!res.ok || data.error) throw new Error(data.error || `HTTP Error: ${res.status}`);\n      if (data.output) {\n        const revised = finalAuditedDocs.replace(selectedParagraph, data.output);\n        setFinalAuditedDocs(revised);\n        if (onAddFileToZip) {\n          onAddFileToZip('DOCUMENTATION.md', revised);\n        }\n        setSelectedParagraph('');\n        setRevisionComment('');\n        setStatus('success');\n        setStatusMsg('Revision updated seamlessly! Saved changes inside your package.');\n      } else {\n        throw new Error(data.error || \"Empty response from editor.\");\n      }\n    } catch (e: any) {\n      \n      setStatus('error');\n      setStatusMsg(`Revision failed: ${e.message}`);\n    } finally {\n      setIsRevising(false);\n    }\n  };\n\n  const copyRef = (text: string) => {\n    navigator.clipboard.writeText(text);\n    setCopied(true);\n    setTimeout(() => setCopied(false), 2500);\n  };\n\n  if (step === 'details') {\n    return (\n      <div className=\"space-y-4 text-left font-mono text-zinc-100\">\n        \n        {/* GROUP 3: INTERVIEW ALIGNMENT DIRECTIVES (Foldable c-card) */}\n        <div className=\"c-card\">\n          <button \n            onClick={() => setInfoFolded(!infoFolded)}\n            className=\"c-card__header\"\n            aria-expanded={!infoFolded}\n          >\n            <span className=\"c-card__title\">\u270d\ufe0f [02] INTERVIEW PROFILE ALIGNMENT DIRECTIVES</span>\n            <span className=\"c-card__toggle\">{infoFolded ? 'OPEN' : 'CLOSE'}</span>\n          </button>\n          \n          {!infoFolded && (\n            <div className=\"c-card__body space-y-4\">\n              <div className=\"space-y-3\">\n                <div>\n                  <label className=\"text-[10px] text-zinc-400 font-black uppercase block tracking-wider\">PROJECT/PRODUCT NAME:</label>\n                  <input \n                    className=\"w-full mt-1 p-2 bg-black border border-zinc-700 text-xs font-bold text-white outline-none focus:border-[#de2626] font-mono\" \n                    placeholder=\"E.g. Express Server Middleware\" \n                    value={details.projectName} \n                    onChange={(e) => setDetails({ ...details, projectName: e.target.value })} \n                  />\n                </div>\n                <div>\n                  <label className=\"text-[10px] text-zinc-400 font-black uppercase block tracking-wider\">CREATOR/DEVELOPER NAME:</label>\n                  <input \n                    className=\"w-full mt-1 p-2 bg-black border border-zinc-700 text-xs font-bold text-white outline-none focus:border-[#de2626] font-mono\" \n                    placeholder=\"E.g.       "import React, { useState } from 'react';\nimport { Loader2, Send, Play, Clipboard, RotateCcw, ChevronRight, Check, Download, Code, Database } from 'lucide-react';\nimport Markdown from 'react-markdown';\nimport { StatusIndicator, StatusType } from './StatusIndicator';\nimport { cn } from '../lib/utils';\nimport { AIProfile } from '../types';\nimport { saveToLibrary, removeFromLibrary } from '../lib/library';\nimport { cleanJsonString, buildHtmlFromJson } from '../lib/jsonHtmlBuilder';\n\ninterface Props {\n  mode: 'single' | 'multi' | 'investigate';\n  contextText: string;\n  selectedModel: string;\n  onAddFileToZip?: (fileName: string, content: string) => void;\n  activeProfile?: AIProfile | null;\n}\n\ninterface PlanStep {\n  number: number;\n  title: string;\n  instruction: string;\n}\n\nexport function DocumentationTool({ mode, contextText, selectedModel, onAddFileToZip, activeProfile }: Props) {\n  const getCompiledInstructions = () => {\n    if (!activeProfile) return undefined;\n    let insts = activeProfile.SystemInstruction || '';\n    if (activeProfile.customFields && activeProfile.customFields.length > 0) {\n      insts += '\\n\\n';\n      activeProfile.customFields.forEach(f => {\n        if (f.key && f.value) {\n          insts += `# ${f.key.trim()}\\n- ${f.value.trim()}\\n\\n`;\n        }\n      });\n    }\n    return insts;\n  };\n  // Shared inputs\n  const [prompt, setPrompt] = useState(\n    mode === 'single' \n      ? \"Write a comprehensive, professional ReadMe for this project. Include installation, clear setup instructions, feature flags, and detailed descriptions of all detected system modules.\"\n      : mode === 'investigate'\n      ? \"Draft a codebase auditing plan covering architecture, security, performance, best practices, and logic bugs etc.\"\n      : \"Draft a 5-step documentation plan outline covering architecture, installation, database/storage strategy, core libraries used, and deployment steps.\"\n  );\n\n  // Status Indicator\n  const [status, setStatus] = useState<StatusType>('idle');\n  const [statusMsg, setStatusMsg] = useState('Workspace initialized. Awaiting instructions.');\n\n  // Single mode outputs\n  const [singleOutput, setSingleOutput] = useState('');\n\n  // Multi-step mode state machine\n  const [stepCount, setStepCount] = useState<number>(5);\n  const [planSteps, setPlanSteps] = useState<PlanStep[]>([]);\n  const [currentStepIndex, setCurrentStepIndex] = useState(0);\n  const [generatedDrafts, setGeneratedDrafts] = useState<Record<number, string>>({});\n  const [currentPartOutput, setCurrentPartOutput] = useState('');\n  const [isAutoRunning, setIsAutoRunning] = useState(false);\n  \n  // Audited Combined Doc\n  const [auditedOutput, setAuditedOutput] = useState('');\n  \n  // Quick Revision Panel\n  const [selectedParagraph, setSelectedParagraph] = useState('');\n  const [revisionComment, setRevisionComment] = useState('');\n  const [isRevising, setIsRevising] = useState(false);\n\n  // Copy success indicator\n  const [copied, setCopied] = useState(false);\n\n  // Collapsible sections\n  const [paramsFolded, setParamsFolded] = useState(false);\n  const [outputFolded, setOutputFolded] = useState(false);\n  const [auditedFolded, setAuditedFolded] = useState(false);\n\n  // Load state from local storage on mount\n  React.useEffect(() => {\n    const savedState = localStorage.getItem(`packcraft_docTool_state_${mode}`);\n    if (savedState) {\n      try {\n        const parsed = JSON.parse(savedState);\n        if (parsed.prompt) setPrompt(parsed.prompt);\n        if (parsed.singleOutput) setSingleOutput(parsed.singleOutput);\n        if (parsed.stepCount !== undefined) setStepCount(parsed.stepCount);\n        if (parsed.planSteps) setPlanSteps(parsed.planSteps);\n        if (parsed.currentStepIndex !== undefined) setCurrentStepIndex(parsed.currentStepIndex);\n        if (parsed.generatedDrafts) setGeneratedDrafts(parsed.generatedDrafts);\n        if (parsed.currentPartOutput) setCurrentPartOutput(parsed.currentPartOutput);\n        if (parsed.auditedOutput) setAuditedOutput(parsed.auditedOutput);\n      } catch (e) {\n        console.warn(\"Failed to parse saved state\", e);\n      }\n    }\n  }, [mode]);\n\n  // Save state to local storage when relevant state changes\n  React.useEffect(() => {\n    const stateToSave = {\n      prompt,\n      singleOutput,\n      stepCount,\n      planSteps,\n      currentStepIndex,\n      generatedDrafts,\n      currentPartOutput,\n      auditedOutput,\n    };\n    localStorage.setItem(`packcraft_docTool_state_${mode}`, JSON.stringify(stateToSave));\n  }, [mode, prompt, singleOutput, stepCount, planSteps, currentStepIndex, generatedDrafts, currentPartOutput, auditedOutput]);\n\n  const startSingleGeneration = async () => {\n    if (!contextText) {\n      alert(\"Please import a project zip archive first to provide context!\");\n      return;\n    }\n    \n    setStatus('sending');\n    setStatusMsg('Transmitting request schema to AI models...');\n    try {\n      setStatus('waiting_reception'); \n      setStatusMsg('Receiving chunks from Gemini and framing ReadMe document...');\n      \n      const res = await fetch('/api/gemini/generate-docs', {\n        method: 'POST',\n        headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },\n        body: JSON.stringify({ \n          prompt, \n          contextText, \n          model: selectedModel,\n          systemInstruction: getCompiledInstructions(),\n          temperature: activeProfile?.Creativity,\n          maxOutputTokens: activeProfile?.MaxResponseTokens\n        })\n      });\n      const data = await res.json();\n      if (!res.ok || data.error) throw new Error(data.error || `HTTP Error: ${res.status}`);\n      if (data.output) {\n        setSingleOutput(data.output);\n        if (onAddFileToZip) {\n          onAddFileToZip('README.md', data.output);\n        }\n        \n        saveToLibrary({\n          id: `single-${Date.now()}`,\n          title: 'README.md',\n          date: new Date().toLocaleString(),\n          content: data.output,\n          type: 'readme',\n          isIncomplete: false\n        });\n\n        setStatus('success');\n        setStatusMsg('Generated comprehensive ReadMe successfully! Added README.md in your zip archive!');\n        setOutputFolded(false);\n      } else {\n        throw new Error(data.error || \"No content generated.\");\n      }\n    } catch (e: any) {\n      \n      setStatus('error');\n      setStatusMsg(`Failure: ${e.message}`);\n    }\n  };\n\n  // Step 1 of Multi-prompt: Draft the Plan Outline\n  const generateMultiStepPlan = async () => {\n    if (!contextText) {\n      alert(\"Please import a project zip archive first to find context!\");\n      return;\n    }\n    \n    setStatus('sending');\n    setStatusMsg(`Drafting ${stepCount}-step detailed plan blueprint...`);\n    try {\n      const planInstructions = mode === 'investigate'\n        ? `Generate exactly ${stepCount} distinct audit steps. Focus heavily on security audits, best practices, structural analysis, performance implications, and bug hunting.
